        [[AdvancedChoices]]
        [[Choice]]

        [[AdvancedAnswers]]
        [[Answer:0]]
        <p>Autonomous bike</p>
        [[Answer:1]]
        <p>Autonomous bike + Public Transit</p>
        [[Answer:2]]
        <p>Keep original choice</p>
                             

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {

                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation

                if (carCoefficient > 0) {

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result

            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

        <p>Keep original choice</p>
                             

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

        <p>Keep original choice</p>
                             

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

        [[Answer:2]]
        <p>Keep original choice</p>
                             

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>

    <script>
        Qualtrics.SurveyEngine.addOnload(function() {
            // Select all elements that need cost calculation
            var costElements = document.querySelectorAll('.calculate-cost');

            costElements.forEach(function(element) {
                // Get the coefficient and time from data attributes
                var coefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-coefficient')) || 0;
                var time = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-time')) || 0;
                var ptCost = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('data-ptcost')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                var carCoefficient = parseFloat(element.getAttribute('car-coefficient')) || 0; // Default to 0 if not provided
                
                // Perform the basic calculation
                var result = coefficient * time;
                
                if (carCoefficient > 0) {
                    result = carCoefficient * time;
                }

                // Add the pt_cost if it exists
                result += ptCost;

                // Update the element's content with the calculated result
                element.innerHTML = result.toFixed(2) + " USD";
            });
        });

    </script>
